Thetford Forest</div></div></div></div><div class="ssrcss-jlwt2c-Divider e8mq1e915"></div></div><div data-component="timestamp-block" class="ssrcss-xza2yt-ComponentWrapper ep2nwvo1"><div><ul role="list" class="ssrcss-j4gvkq-MetadataStripContainer eh44mf03"><div class="ssrcss-13nu8ri-GroupChildrenForWrapping eh44mf02"><li role="listitem" class="ssrcss-30fcoe-MetadataStripItem eh44mf01"><div class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Published</div><div class="ssrcss-m5j4pi-MetadataContent eh44mf00"><span class="ssrcss-1pvwv4b-MetadataSnippet e4wm5bw3"><span class="ssrcss-1if1g9v-MetadataText e4wm5bw1"><time data-testid="timestamp" dateTime="2024-06-10T00:59:15.619Z">6 hours ago</time></span></span></div></li></div></ul></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-uf6wea-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Scientists sampling DNA in the air to monitor the spread of deadly diseases said their work could help make food prices cheaper.</b></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The Earlham Institute in Norwich said its air sampler processes detect bacteria, viruses and other micro-organisms - which pose a threat to plants, animals and humans - more quickly and accurately than other techniques.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">This could help farmers grow crops more cheaply and efficiently as they would not need to use as many chemicals.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">It could also transform environmental conservation work as well as public health measures.</p></div></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-xza2yt-ComponentWrapper ep2nwvo1"><figure class="ssrcss-8589xk-StyledFigure e34k3c23"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-1hjcqmo-Placeholder etlorgc0"><span><noscript><picture><source srcSet="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/news/240/cpsprodpb/33e7/live/b6c73df0-0a35-11ef-9517-0f5643a5629b.jpg.webp 240w, 976w" width="2048" height="1151.8218097447796" class="ssrcss-11yxrdo-Image edrdn950"/></picture></noscript></span></span><span role="text" class="ssrcss-tvuve5-StyledFigureCopyright e34k3c20"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image source, </span>Martin Giles/BBC</span></div><figcaption class="ssrcss-1mget3o-StyledFigureCaption e34k3c22"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image caption, </span><div spacing="6" class="ssrcss-y7krbn-Stack e1y4nx260"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The scientists have named their air samplers after characters from Pride and Prejudice</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-uf6wea-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">All living things are constantly shedding bits of DNA into their surroundings.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mia Berelson, who is a PhD student at the institute, says this technique gives us an idea of what is living where, and when, very quickly.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;Each device works like a really big hoover. They suck in over 200 litres of air per minute,&quot; she says.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;The air goes through the filter, and anything in the air - like bits of bacteria, skin cells, bits of pollen - that all gets stuck on the filter.&quot;</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">That DNA will then be sequenced and a profile will be created of all the different organisms detected in the area.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The Earlham Institute has been sampling the air near farmers&#x27; fields for several years but is now also sampling coastal, forest and city locations too.</p></div></div><div data-component="image-block" class="ssrcss-xza2yt-ComponentWrapper ep2nwvo1"><figure class="ssrcss-8589xk-StyledFigure e34k3c23"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-fmt1c3-Placeholder etlorgc0"><span><noscript><picture><source class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image source, </span>Earlham Institute</span></div><figcaption class="ssrcss-1mget3o-StyledFigureCaption e34k3c22"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image caption, </span><div spacing="6" class="ssrcss-y7krbn-Stack e1y4nx260"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Two devices are in place at Brancaster on the Norfolk coast</p></div></figcaption></figure></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-uf6wea-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Eight samplers have been placed across Norfolk including Brancaster, Norwich city centre, Thetford Forest and at <a href="https://www.suffolkwildlifetrust.org/carlton" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0">Carlton &amp; Oulton Marshes<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a> in Suffolk.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">There are many more now in Cambridgeshire, Lincolnshire and Oxfordshire.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The team switches on the devices at the same time for one hour and will repeat the experiment every three months to get an idea of seasonal changes.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The full results will be analysed in Spring 2025.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Post-doctoral scientist Darren Heavens said: &quot;Food will be cheaper.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;If we inform the farmer that there&#x27;s a pathogen in the air, he can take a more targeted approach when it comes to spraying [chemicals].</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;If he only has to spray one, he&#x27;ll save money. If the pathogen&#x27;s not there at all, he  won&#x27;t have to spray at all, again saving money.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">&quot;If he can save money, that can be passed on and the customer will get a cheaper product.&quot;</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But the research has only just begun, so it will be a while before any difference may be noticed at the checkouts.</p></div></div><div data-component="text-block" class="ssrcss-uf6wea-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0"><div class="ssrcss-7uxr49-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">Follow East of England news on </i><a href="https://www.facebook.com/bbcnewseast/" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0"><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">Facebook</i><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">, </i><a href="https://www.instagram.com/bbceastofengland/" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0"><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">Instagram</i><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2"> and </i><a href="https://twitter.com/lookeast" class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0"><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">X</i><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a><i class="ssrcss-xbdn93-ItalicText e5tfeyi2">.
